anb_define_long_lived_heir = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { heirAge = $age$ }
		export_to_variable = {
			which = birthDate
			value = trigger_value:is_year
		}
		
		subtract_variable = {
			which = birthDate
			which = heirAge
		}
